## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Test Execution]) --> Init[Initialize TripLegValidator]
    Init --> Test1{test_validate_put}
    Init --> Test2{test_validate_put_with_not_null_id}
    Init --> Test3{test_validate_put_with_missing_fields}
    
    Test1 --> Create1[Create TripLeg with all required fields]
    Create1 --> SetAll1[Set all properties: solution_id, owner_org, carrier_org, destination, origin, shipment_number, creator_shipment_id, sequence_number, type]
    SetAll1 --> Valid1[Call validator.validate PUT]
    Valid1 --> Pass1[No exception - Test passes]
    
    Test2 --> Create2[Create TripLeg with ID]
    Create2 --> SetAll2[Set all required properties]
    SetAll2 --> Valid2[Call validator.validate PUT]
    Valid2 --> Pass2[No exception - Test passes]
    
    Test3 --> Create3[Create empty TripLeg]
    Create3 --> Check1[Validate - Expect all fields missing error]
    Check1 --> AddSol[Add solution_id]
    AddSol --> Check2[Validate - Expect remaining fields error]
    Check2 --> AddOwner[Add owner_organization_fv_id]
    AddOwner --> Check3[Validate - Expect remaining fields error]
    Check3 --> AddCarrier[Add carrier_organization_fv_id]
    AddCarrier --> Check4[Validate - Expect remaining fields error]
    Check4 --> AddDest[Add destination_location_code]
    AddDest --> Check5[Validate - Expect remaining fields error]
    Check5 --> AddOrigin[Add origin_location_code]
    AddOrigin --> Check6[Validate - Expect shipment and sequence error]
    Check6 --> AddCreator[Add creator_shipment_id]
    AddCreator --> Check7[Validate - Expect sequence_number error]
    Check7 --> AddSeq[Add sequence_number]
    AddSeq --> Check8[Validate - Expect type error]
    Check8 --> AddType[Add type=PLANNED and shipment_number]
    AddType --> Check9[Validate - Success]
    Check9 --> Pass3[Test passes]
    
    Pass1 --> End([Tests Complete])
    Pass2 --> End
    Pass3 --> End
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> EmptyTripLeg
    EmptyTripLeg --> HasSolutionId: Add solution_id
    HasSolutionId --> HasOwnerOrg: Add owner_organization_fv_id
    HasOwnerOrg --> HasCarrier: Add carrier_organization_fv_id
    HasCarrier --> HasDestination: Add destination_location_code
    HasDestination --> HasOrigin: Add origin_location_code
    HasOrigin --> HasShipmentId: Add creator_shipment_id OR shipment_number
    HasShipmentId --> HasSequence: Add sequence_number
    HasSequence --> ValidTripLeg: Add valid type (PLANNED/ACTUAL)
    ValidTripLeg --> [*]: Validation Success
    
    EmptyTripLeg --> ValidationError: Validate
    HasSolutionId --> ValidationError: Validate
    HasOwnerOrg --> ValidationError: Validate
    HasCarrier --> ValidationError: Validate
    HasDestination --> ValidationError: Validate
    HasOrigin --> ValidationError: Validate
    HasShipmentId --> ValidationError: Validate
    HasSequence --> ValidationError: Validate (no type)
    
    ValidationError --> [*]: Test Assertion
```
